***шрам.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шрам.html>шрам</a> (5516)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk"><a href = vnd.unilang:шрам.html>шрам</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šram</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">szram</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">szrama</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">schramme</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">schramm</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Schramme</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шрам.html>шрам</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šram</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шрам.html>шра́ма</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шрам.html>шра́мы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шрам.html>шра́мов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>scar, cicatrix (a permanent mark on the skin sometimes caused by the healing of a wound)</li></ol>

***шредер.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шредер.html>шре́дер</a> (17594)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">shredder</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шредер.html>шре́дер</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šrɛ́dɛr</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шредер.html>шре́дера</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шредер.html>шре́деры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шредер.html>шре́деров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>shredder (machine that tears up objects into smaller pieces)</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Schrift</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">writing; font</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:штамм.html>штамм</a> (29505)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Stamm</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штамм.html>штамм</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">štamm</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штамм.html>шта́мма</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штамм.html>шта́ммы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штамм.html>шта́ммов</a></b>)

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Stampfe</i>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штамп.html>штамп</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">štamp</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штамп.html>шта́мпа</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штамп.html>шта́мпы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штамп.html>шта́мпов</a></b>)

***штат.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:штат.html>штат</a> (2621)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Staat</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">state, country</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">stāt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">staet</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">stātus</i>. The semantic development was influenced by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">état</i> from the same Latin source.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штат.html>штат</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">štat</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штат.html>шта́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штат.html>шта́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штат.html>шта́тов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>state <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a political division, e.g. a US state</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>staff <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">personnel</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штат.html>штат</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">štat</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штатный.html>шта́тный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">štátnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>staff, personnel
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:штатный.html>шта́тное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:расписание.html>расписа́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>štátnoje</b> raspisánije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">staff list; manning table; salary schedule</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>staff
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:штатный.html>шта́тный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:преподаватель.html>преподава́тель</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>štátnyj</b> prepodavátelʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">staff teacher/professor</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:штатный.html>шта́тный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:работник.html>рабо́тник</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>štátnyj</b> rabótnik</i> ― <span class="e-translation">staff member</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>standard, regular, normal
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:штатный.html>шта́тный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:режим.html>режи́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>štátnyj</b> režím</i> ― <span class="e-translation">standard/nominal/normal mode</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>routine, nonemergency
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:штатный.html>шта́тная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ситуация.html>ситуа́ция</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>štátnaja</b> situácija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">normal/routine situation; non-emergency</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">normal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нормальный.html>норма́льный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">normálʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ординарный.html>ордина́рный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ordinárnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***штопать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:штопать.html>што́пать</a> (24190)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">stoppen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to darn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">stopfen</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штопать.html>што́пать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">štópatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заштопать.html>зашто́пать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to darn (stitch with thread)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:штормовой.html>штормово́й</a> (22945)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шторм.html>шторм</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">štorm</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ово́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штормовой.html>штормово́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">štormovój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> storm
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:штормовой.html>штормова́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:волна.html>волна́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>štormovája</b> volná</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>storm</b> surge</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>storm</b> wave</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li>stormy</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***штрафной.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:штрафной.html>штрафно́й</a> (10933)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штраф.html>штраф</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">štraf</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-но́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штрафной.html>штрафно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">štrafnój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> penalty</li>
<li>penal</li>
<li>consisting of penalised soldiers, sportsmen, etc.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штрафной.html>штрафно́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:удар.html>уда́р</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">štrafnój udár</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штраф.html>штраф</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">štraf</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штрафовать.html>штрафова́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">štrafovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оштрафовать.html>оштрафова́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">oštrafovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штрафной.html>штрафно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">štrafnój</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штрафной.html>штрафно́го</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штрафной.html>штрафны́е</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штрафной.html>штрафны́х</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate<span class="ib-comma">,</span> military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> soldier sent to a penal military battalion</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate<span class="ib-comma">,</span> sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a player who has been penalized</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate<span class="ib-comma">,</span> sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> penalty kick, free throw, etc.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:учиться.html>учи́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:забивать.html>забива́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:штрафной.html>штрафны́е</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nádo učítʹsja zabivátʹ <b>štrafnýje</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">You need to practice making your <b>penalty kicks</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***штрафовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:штрафовать.html>штрафова́ть</a> (23562)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">strafen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to punish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Composed of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штраф.html>штраф</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">štraf</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штрафовать.html>штрафова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">štrafovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оштрафовать.html>оштрафова́ть</a></b>)
</p>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Strich</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штрих.html>штрих</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">štrix</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штрих.html>штриха́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штрих.html>штрихи́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штрих.html>штрихо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>stroke, hatch, hachures, dash
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:штрих.html>штрих</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:знак.html>зна́ка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>štrix</b> znáka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">character stroke</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:штрих.html>штрих</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шкала.html>шкалы́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>štrix</b> škalý</i> ― <span class="e-translation">scale line/mark</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>trait, feature, detail
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:характерный.html>характе́рный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:штрих.html>штрих</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">xaraktérnyj <b>štrix</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">characteristic trait</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***штука.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:штука.html>шту́ка</a> (1647)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">sztuka</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">piece</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, in turn from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Stück</i>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">shtick</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штука.html>шту́ка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">štúka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штука.html>шту́ки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штука.html>шту́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штука.html>шту́к</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>piece, each (in counting items)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свеча.html>свеча́</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одна́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:штука.html>шту́ка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Svečá — odná <b>štúka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">Candle — one each (= one candle)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>thing
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>Что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:штука.html>шту́ка</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Što éto za <b>štúka</b>?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">What sort of <b>thing</b> is this?</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>Вот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:штука.html>шту́ка</a></b>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vot tak <b>štúka</b>!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">What a mess!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> thousand
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:штука.html>шту́ку</a></b> ба́ксов <a href = vnd.unilang:должный.html>до́лжен</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On mne <b>štúku</b> báksov dólžen</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He owes me a thousand bucks.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">aviation</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Stuka <i>(German Junkers Ju 87 dive bomber)</i></li></ol>

***штукатурка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:штукатурка.html>штукату́рка</a> (11671)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штукатурка.html>штукату́рка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">štukatúrka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штукатурка.html>штукату́рки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штукатурка.html>штукату́рки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штукатурка.html>штукату́рок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>stucco, plaster</li>
<li>plastering</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloqial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> ironical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> heavy make-up, slap</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:штурм.html>штурм</a> (6155)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Sturm</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">assault, attack, storm</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штурм.html>штурм</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šturm</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штурм.html>шту́рма</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штурм.html>шту́рмы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штурм.html>шту́рмов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>storm, storming of something</li>
<li>assault <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a violent onset or attack</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взять.html>взять</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:штурм.html>шту́рмом</a></b> что́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vzjatʹ <b>štúrmom</b> štó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take something <b>by storm</b></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Not to be confused with <b><a href = vnd.unilang:шторм.html>шторм</a></b>, a storm as a weather event.
